 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Road Rebel                                                    บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction to RCN #20                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am writing this to say a few words about RCN and how people treat   บ
 บ  us.  First of all, when you see an article that rips on someone or a      บ
 บ  group, and you don't like it.  Take it up with the author!!!  If it       บ
 บ  isn't written by Rebel Chicken, Hitex or I then don't nag us about it!    บ
 บ  Also, if you have a problem with something written about you or a group,  บ
 บ  WRITE A REBUTTLE!  Don't sit there and bitch at us in the channel, it     บ
 บ  doesn't do shit.  I came to #RCN today, and all I heard was bitching      บ
 บ  because someone said something mean about a group.  WELL, if you are a    บ
 บ  group member and your group gets made fun of, take it on the chin, be a   บ
 บ  man.  We have and will make fun of A LOT of people, most of it is just    บ
 บ  FUN and in MAD RCN, and people realize this and get over it.  If you      บ
 บ  come in and bitch at us, it makes us want to rip you some more.  Ok       บ
 บ  enough of this.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, this is for the people that come in and say "SEND ME THE NEWEST  บ
 บ  RCN!"  You don't have to beg!!!!  Before you nag people for it try this.  บ
 บ  Look in the channel for someone named *dcc (anythingdcc).  If they exist  บ
 บ  type this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc list"  If they list that they have it type  บ
 บ  this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc send #<pack@>"                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      OK!!  NOW, if there isn't a DCC in the channel look at the topic.     บ
 บ  It will usually have an FTP or Web page adrress!  If they aren't there,   บ
 บ  then ask.  Please don't just come in and BEG. It is very unbecoming.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, for people that want to write for RCN, you don't have to ask    บ
 บ  for an RCN app.  Just write something and send it to me.  If it is good   บ
 บ  we use it, if not, well.. we don't.  However, our editors are very        บ
 บ  patient and they will try to unscramble any submission, regardless of     บ
 บ  your English skills.  Also, we readily accept submissions written in      บ
 บ  French, Hebrew, Spanish, or Swedish.  Don't worry, we'll get it           บ
 บ  translated!  (Of course, we still prefer English!)  If you can keep       บ
 บ  submitting to RCN you will become a member.  But don't ask what the       บ
 บ  topic should be, if we had all the topics we could write the whole        บ
 บ  magazine, the topics are the hard part!                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ


                                         
                   ฿ ฐฐ฿  r c n  ฐ   ฿ฐ฿ฐ
                 ฐ    ฿฿฿       ฿  ฿฿฿   ฿฿
       ฿฿฿       ฐ฿   ฿   ฿฿      ฐ    
 ฿   ฿ฐ ฐ  ฐ ฐ ฐฐ ฐฐ฿฿ ฐฐฐฐ ฐ ฐฐฐ
฿฿฿฿฿฿     ฿฿   ฐ฿฿       ฿ฐ   ฿ ฿฿฿
 ฿฿       ฿฿   ฐ  ฿   ฿฿฿฿    ฿  ฿      ฿ฐ฿
    ฿฿฿฿฿  ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿             ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿ฐ     ฿
                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am Rio & Ken, this is the first time I'm writing to RCN, so let me  บ
 บ  introduce myself.  I'm a bbs trader that has been around in the scene     บ
 บ  for about 1.5 years now.  Right now I'm in Razor 1911, Rapier, Mortality  บ
 บ  and that's all.  Now that you know who I am, I can speak.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I wrote this letter to talk about your magazine, I really think it    บ
 บ  sucks.  The thing is, I'm not the only one.  There are many reasons for   บ
 บ  that, and well, I'll start explaining.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First, as I see it, your purpose in the scene (as a scene magazine)   บ
 บ  is to help the scene in many ways and to supply scene-news/gossip to      บ
 บ  scene-people weekly.  Now, that's cool and stuff, and you know, it's      บ
 บ  thoughtful and caring and all.  But because of your blind eyes, you       บ
 บ  don't see what you actually do.  Your magazine's publicity is starting    บ
 บ  to be pretty huge, and the magazine is falling to a lot of men's          บ
 บ  computers - now it may seem really cool from your side (having great      บ
 บ  publicity), but I don't know if you are aware of the fact that all of     บ
 บ  this actually REALLY ruins the scene because of the publicty the          บ
 บ  magazine is getting to a lot of non-scene people, and even some           บ
 บ  anti-scene people.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As you know the magazine contains A LOT of information about the      บ
 บ  scene, and some of it even secret shit that is illegal.  I'm writing      บ
 บ  this to remind you that the scene is SUPPOSED to be UNDERGROUND.  Some    บ
 บ  of the actions in it are illegal, and that's why publishing a magazine    บ
 บ  like yours, is dangerous - for you, for me, and for the whole scene.      บ
 บ  You know, the ONLY good thing I saw in your magazine was the revealing    บ
 บ  of this lame Chris Carter, but as I'm thinking, I'm concluding that your  บ
 บ  magazine is exactly like Chris Carter, you're a big source of             บ
 บ  information about the scene and about its illegal actions.  The amazing   บ
 บ  thing is that you even mention a lot of handles/names/email-addreses and  บ
 บ  lots of more revealing stuff!!  I just can't understand how blind all of  บ
 บ  you RCN-staff-people are and you just can't see how you ruin us all.  I   บ
 บ  think it's already happend once with DRAPPER's site.  All I'm suggesting  บ
 บ  is, if you want to continue running this lame-tragedy-magazine, sure, go  บ
 บ  ahead, who'll stop you, just try doing it in a lot more quiet way and     บ
 บ  don't reveal in your magazine so much, but just one thing, don't ever     บ
 บ  say you're helping the scene, as I said, you all are doing exactly the    บ
 บ  opposite!                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So after explaining why your magazine is lame I wanted to ask you,    บ
 บ  no no, to DEMAND from you that I not to see MY handle/name on your        บ
 บ  magazine EVER in ANY of the issues in the future, that includes the TOP   บ
 บ  10 COURIERS (even if I should be there), and I do that for my own         บ
 บ  safety, because GOD knows what MORE you will publish about me except for  บ
 บ  the handle, and by the way, I sugggest that all people that care for      บ
 บ  themselves demand the same thing!  Again, if I'll ever see my name, I     บ
 บ  will personally take it as my mission in the scene to take you all and    บ
 บ  your magazine DOWN the drain.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway dude, that's all, I put it all out of my heart, I hope you'll  บ
 บ  pay good attnetion to what I wrote and will have the brain to fix         บ
 บ  everything right.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I just felt compelled to write you guys after going through RCN #19.  บ
 บ  You guys did a great job!  Well, let's not make this into another         บ
 บ  dumbass "great work" e-mail.  I have a few things to comment on, but      บ
 บ  feel free to ignore me.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is my take on the current warez scene situation, from the point  บ
 บ  of view of someone who hasn't been involved with it for a few years. I'm  บ
 บ  what you guys would call an art scener.  I used to be into the local 604  บ
 บ  (my home AC) warez scene, 2-3 years ago, but I moved into the art scene   บ
 บ  about two years ago and never left :).  Just to give you a little         บ
 บ  background on myself, I started out as a local art pack courier.          บ
 บ  Pathetic, eh?  Somehow, that led me into drawing for a local art group    บ
 บ  (Mistigris), where I developed my ANSI skills.  Since then, I've become   บ
 บ  a pretty good artist (if I can actually say that modestly :), proficient  บ
 บ  in a wide range of artistic media (ANSI, RIP, VGA, and a little ASCII)    บ
 บ  and have gone through a series of small-to-large groups (Mistigris, WBT,  บ
 บ  Integrity, Union, Flatline, mOp, iCE, and finally Fire, which I am now a  บ
 บ  senior staffer in).                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As I progressed into the art scene, I became less and less involved   บ
 บ  in the warez scene; of course, I picked up the odd Ware or two, but       บ
 บ  never to the extent that a lot of guys are doing now.  I really lost      บ
 บ  contact with my warez roots.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Within the last few weeks, I've gotten a little more involved in the  บ
 บ  warez scene again.  It all started off when I was sitting peacefully on   บ
 บ  #Fire, talking to my buds; in cruises a courier, asking for someone to    บ
 บ  draw him a DIZ.  I volunteered.  Actually, I just graduated, so I was     บ
 บ  looking for some warez to occupy my free time; I grabbed the opportunity  บ
 บ  to get myself some :).  You see, a lot of us art scene guys are           บ
 บ  warez-deprived.  We don't see many warez anymore, unless we're totally    บ
 บ  into the warez scene.  So I asked the courier if we could wrangle a       บ
 บ  trade for warez or something.  He sent me to his leader, a guy called     บ
 บ  Druggy (whom I had never encountered before, but he seems to be somewhat  บ
 บ  of a fixture in the warez scene :), who had just started up a new         บ
 บ  courier group, The Cartel.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I talked to him, and he asked me to show him some of my         บ
 บ  artwork.  In a sense, you guys are art-deprived :).  I sent him over      บ
 บ  some of my old junk, and he loved it.  Kept asking me to send him more,   บ
 บ  actually.  That was pretty weird, since most of the art scene guys don't  บ
 บ  ask anymore; my work is pretty readily available in art packs released    บ
 บ  monthly, such as the ACiD Acquisition, the monthly iCEpack, and the Fire  บ
 บ  Combustion.  Most packs release monthly, filled to the brim with artwork  บ
 บ  like mine. He asked me to fill out an app to his group and to draw some   บ
 บ  stuff for them.  I saw this as a great opportunity to fill my harddrive   บ
 บ  up with crap, so I said "sure, what the hell."  Within minutes I was      บ
 บ  opped on #Cartel, sitting there, chatting with warez guys I'd never met   บ
 บ  before, many of them questioning me about what kind of artwork I did.     บ
 บ  To make a long story short, I sent a bunch of them my old work, and they  บ
 บ  got to know me a bit through my artwork :).  I drew up a nifty colour     บ
 บ  member list, and got access on a few warez sites. I'm a happy camper      บ
 บ  now; it doesn't take much to satisfy me, warez-wise :)                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since then (this was about a week or two ago), I've gotten more       บ
 บ  involved with the warez scene. Druggy kindly sent me Issue #17 of RCN,    บ
 บ  telling me that I was insane never to have read it before. He seemed to   บ
 บ  think RCN was the best mag ever released :).  I thought to myself "It's   บ
 บ  a warez mag. It can't be that great."  Boy, was I wrong.  Again, great    บ
 บ  effort guys.  It rocks.  RCN shines in comparison to most art scene       บ
 บ  emags.  Three things shocked me the most about RCN.  Here they are, in    บ
 บ  order :                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) The fact that you guys release weekly.  This seems physically     บ
 บ          impossible to me, an art scene lameass who never knew mags could  บ
 บ          release any faster than monthly.  Art scene mags are all          บ
 บ          under-staffed, and release monthly if they're _lucky_.  The fact  บ
 บ          that you guys manage to release weekly, and actualy ON TIME blew  บ
 บ          my mind.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) The quantity of stuff you guys manage to collect on a regular     บ
 บ          basis for inclusion into RCN.  It's scary that the warez scene    บ
 บ          is so active :).  You guys manage to scrape up more articles,     บ
 บ          interviews and editorials weekly than most art mags came come up  บ
 บ          with in 2-3 months.  Jesus!                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) The amount of following RCN has.  Last week, just before the      บ
 บ          release of RCN #18, the guys on #Cartel were going nuts about     บ
 บ          how long RCN had been delayed.  At the time, I had no idea you    บ
 บ          guys released WEEKLY.  I thought to myself, based on my           บ
 บ          knowledge of art scene mags, "what, they must be a coupla days    บ
 บ          late, right?"  WRONG.  A bloody HOUR late, and everyone was       บ
 บ          ranting and raving about how late you guys were.  Shut the hell   บ
 บ          up, you whining freaks :).  You obviously haven't been in the     บ
 บ          art scene before.  We have mags that release a MONTH late, and    บ
 บ          no one really complains, due to the utter LACK of cooperation     บ
 บ          from anyone.  An HOUR late?  You whiners should be ashamed of     บ
 บ          yourselves.  I mean, it's already a major accomplishment, in my   บ
 บ          eyes, that you managed to release weekly at all.  That's already  บ
 บ          a BIG plus for RCN.  But whining because the mag was an HOUR      บ
 บ          late in coming out? Gimme a break.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since then I've been faithfully reading each issue of RCN I find,     บ
 บ  "cover-to-cover", so-to-speak.  I'm constantly impressed by the amount    บ
 บ  of quality and humourous material you guys manage to scrape up; awesome   บ
 บ  job, guys.  The coding is excellent, the intro and closing graphics are   บ
 บ  great, and the content just plain rocks.  I myself run an art webzine,    บ
 บ  called "netherwOrld", (which is temporarily down, because I can't find a  บ
 บ  server to house it ;( ) but I strive to keep it updated as regularly as   บ
 บ  you guys keep RCN updated.  Again, I'm REALLY impressed.  The fact that   บ
 บ  your staff is so large and cooperative is a major plus, and that you      บ
 บ  have your own web domain (haven't looked at it yet, but I will today) is  บ
 บ  great too.  You must have a huge distribution.  The only thing I don't    บ
 บ  like (yes, I actually don't like something in RCN!) about the mag is      บ
 บ  your menuset.  Sorry to say, but for a mag as good as RCN, they really    บ
 บ  bite!                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Cereal                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear An Aspiring Coder,                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Unfortunately when we looked around for protected mode source all we  บ
 บ  ever saw was "register me" or it would die in 30 days.  So we decided to  บ
 บ  screw protected mode.  RCN runs off of a built-in overlay file.  The      บ
 บ  overlays are stored within the main EXE so there is no need to have       บ
 บ  extraneous outside data files.  The configuration is also stored in       บ
 บ  several bytes within the main EXE.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Xenon                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I would like to use this chance to reply to an editorial by a person  บ
 บ  named Joker, posted in the 19th issue of RCN.  There he said something    บ
 บ  about the games scene dying out, and that he personally thought that it   บ
 บ  was no big loss, as the utils scene is more important.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I couldn't disagree more.  The fact is that the reason why the        บ
 บ  number of good games in the scene today always exceeds the amount of      บ
 บ  good utilities by far is because it is much easier to come up with a new  บ
 บ  concept in gaming than in utilities.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The thing is, after playing Doom and beating all the levels ten       บ
 บ  times without loading game a single time, people are still willing to     บ
 บ  play Doom 2.  But once you have already found the perfect communications  บ
 บ  program, or the best Dos shell, you really don't care  about any new      บ
 บ  comm proggies, or Dos shells that come out.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I think that if the CD releases were to kill the games scene       บ
 บ  (which I doubt, as so much room in them is taken up by the movies and     บ
 บ  voices that are so easy for our expert groups to rip out) whatever would  บ
 บ  be left of it, would be pretty boring, and people will soon lose their    บ
 บ  interest in it.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Netman                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For about a month now, all I've been hearing is how my friends keep   บ
 บ  getting busted for doing jack, and quite frankly, I am sick of it!  Dr.   บ
 บ  Jekyll was the first of whom was taken by them.  I valued his             บ
 บ  companionship greatly due to the fact he was always the first one to      บ
 บ  greet me when I logged on, and was always ready to help me find whatever  บ
 บ  I needed, not to mention getting me honorary ops a few times :) Dr.       บ
 บ  Jekyll.. if you ever read this, thank you for everything.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Dr. Jekyll was busted, and I was feeling kinda down.  We all go       บ
 บ  through it, but it passes, and I dismissed it as just something that      บ
 บ  happened.  I myself stopped hacking a while ago, but I still felt         บ
 บ  comfortable that if I ever wanted to return, I would be pretty safe.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Then, recently, OoZiE, another of my friends, was busted for using    บ
 บ  *ONE* hacked aimnet.com account!  To this end I was strongly              บ
 บ  disappointed.. For a full day, I sat at my terminal and wondered what     บ
 บ  was going on, and seriously considered dropping out of the scene.  After  บ
 บ  all, I have a future right now (for the most part) and don't want to      บ
 บ  blow it just for some stupid games and apps, no matter how good they may  บ
 บ  seem to be.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After sitting there and contemplating, I went and played a game of    บ
 บ  the Quake beta which just shot those preminitions away.  I'd like to      บ
 บ  think I didn't waste that time, and I'm glad I'm writing to you.  We are  บ
 บ  the future, and if we stick together, we cannot be contained.  I hate to  บ
 บ  bitch about the profiteering made on the net, but fact is that there are  บ
 บ  hundreds, perhaps thousands of corporate morons sitting there trying to   บ
 บ  find ways to make MORE money for their corporations from the Internet,    บ
 บ  and to them, an obstacle is the lack of control in CyberSpace.  I think   บ
 บ  that everytime there is a bust, every H/P/A/C'er, and those in the warez  บ
 บ  scene, should take note and pay them a moment of silence.  One day,       บ
 บ  unless I'm careful, I will be taken down, fined, and probably jailed.     บ
 บ  If you're not careful, the next one down might be you.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Orange Sun                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : MGD                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Amnesia Falls!            Affiliation : ex-Amnesia Senior    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : MGD (The Midnight Gravedigger), you were a senior of GODS (Guild    บ
 บ        of Distributors) and when GODS switched its name to Amnesia, you    บ
 บ        became an Amnesia senior, but you recently left Amnesia, why is     บ
 บ        that so?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : I left Amnesia because there are many problems there now, I mean    บ
 บ        like any one that wants to join they can join these days, Amnesia   บ
 บ        standards have been lowered since before we went to GODS and then   บ
 บ        pulled out.  Davan is about to retire and Frost went to Damage.     บ
 บ        Prozac is gone, and Shafter is in Chicago for the summer, which     บ
 บ        doesn't leave Amnesia with much these days, they got a few          บ
 บ        newbies, who can't show respect to people that kept the group       บ
 บ        alive before they were even on the Internet.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : But what about the council members such as Lester and David &       บ
 บ        Goliath?  Are they not respectable enough to be able to keep the    บ
 บ        group together?  Or are they too no longer capable of running       บ
 บ        Amnesia as a decent group?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Lester is not around much, and David & Goliath is trying to run     บ
 บ        Amnesia like its his utils group The Corporation.  Many others      บ
 บ        (names willl not be revealed) and I have a great amount of respect  บ
 บ        for Lester, he is one of the most powerful people on the Internet,  บ
 บ        and he usuallly kept things in order when he was around, but he     บ
 บ        comes on like 15 minutes every other day now, and with a group      บ
 บ        like Amnesia that is certainly not enough.  As for David &          บ
 บ        Goliath, no comment.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned that Frost left Amnesia for Damage?  What's his new   บ
 บ        position in Damage?  Did he leave Amnesia for the same reasons you  บ
 บ        too are leaving?  What part did Frost play in Amnesia's success?    บ
 บ        In other words, is he THAT important?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Frost is certainly in my mind a great rising star in the field of   บ
 บ        Internet couriering.  He is getting better and better daily, he     บ
 บ        left Amnesia for Damage basically because there are fights every    บ
 บ        day in channel #Amnesia.  He he was a KEY FACTOR in AMNESiA's       บ
 บ        sucess.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : History does repeat itself.  Amnesia first split off of Malice in   บ
 บ        February because of fights, and now Damage is splitting away from   บ
 บ        Amnesia.  Do you believe that my statement on how history repeats   บ
 บ        itself is true?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Damage split when Digital split into GODS, and Rapier split out of  บ
 บ        Amnesia, which is correct.  Amnesia did split out of MALICE         บ
 บ        because of fights.  Fights are what the splits start off of, and    บ
 บ        when a figure in the group leaves, many others think of leaving     บ
 บ        too.  Yes, your statement is true except for the part where Damage  บ
 บ        split from Amnesia, it split from Digital.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : After Malice's fall in February, it has never been the same group   บ
 บ        because it could not maintain its courier prowess.  Do you believe  บ
 บ        that Amnesia has taken its fall as well, and is pretty much done    บ
 บ        for, unless something short of a miracle comes and saves the        บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Well, I am not too sure about that one, you can look at Malice and  บ
 บ        see from #1 to practically dead, it has happened to many groups,    บ
 บ        and at this point almost nothing can save the group.  About         บ
 บ        Amnesia, I really can't say because Amnesia still has some good     บ
 บ        Internet couriers and only time will tell.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned earlier that when figure heads leave a group, others  บ
 บ        lose faith and want to leave as well.  Have any other Amnesia       บ
 บ        couriers left Amnesia as a result of your departure?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Well on that I would call it as me and Frost left together, and     บ
 บ        because of this nuisance, Davan might be retiring, I have gotten    บ
 บ        messages from people still in AMNESiA telling me "you know another  บ
 บ        group that will take me, I would leave AMNESiA but as of now I      บ
 บ        don't have any where else to go."                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : We know that Frost left Amnesia to join Damage, but which courier   บ
 บ        group will you be joining?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : I really can't say yet, I have talked to Eagle 1 of RiSC (Rise in   บ
 บ        Superior Couriering) and he told me to talk to him when he gets     บ
 บ        back on Wednesday or Thursday after his upcoming buisness trip      บ
 บ        that he has already left for.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I recall in that in RCN issue #18, a log file was shown where you   บ
 บ        said that RiSC hates you?  And that you would never be able to      บ
 บ        join that group?  Is that not true?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : RiSC doesn't hate me, I had some actions in Amnesia towards RiSC    บ
 บ        but that was only because of pride in Amnesia which I have totally  บ
 บ        lost completely, as it is for RiSC sure I would join now, if I was  บ
 บ        given the chance.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What were these actions?  Did you try to steal sites from RiSC?     บ
 บ        You said in RCN Issue #18, "I say we steal LA, Enigma, and Beyond   บ
 บ        Akira from RiSC."                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : That was just jibberish because I was still mad on how BBX of       บ
 บ        Amnesia was taken by RiSC, yet that is long forgotten.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Oh, okay, it's long forgotten.  Two weeks is a long time.  Anyway,  บ
 บ        what are your feelings toward Amnesia now that you are no longer a  บ
 บ        part of it?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : I could care less about Amnesia, they don't know how to respect     บ
 บ        people that kept the group alive when every one was inactive.  I    บ
 บ        still have friends there that I care for, but much of the group is  บ
 บ        deteriorating.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How did they fail in giving you the respect you feel you deserve?   บ
 บ        I assume the lack of respect was directed at you, correct?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MGD : Well a little while back before GODS, a little after that Amnesia   บ
 บ        vs. Digital courier competition, I was the ONLY Internet trader     บ
 บ        actually performing when the others were gone with their excuses,   บ
 บ        so I was keeping Amnesia alive, I also trained and formed that      บ
 บ        current Internet team they have with an exception of a few people,  บ
 บ        and in my point of view that certainly should get me some respect.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Ante                      Interviewee : Tym                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Blizzard on Piracy        Affiliation : Blizzard Programmer  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What does Blizzard do to prevent software piracy?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Well, there are a few different things.  The main thing is to       บ
 บ        eliminate as many reasons to pirate the software as possible.       บ
 บ        There's a lot of people out there who get pirated games because     บ
 บ        they don't want to spend money on something they know nothing       บ
 บ        about.  Besides the usual shareware, we also provide spawning       บ
 บ        technology, that allows multiple people to play each other off one  บ
 บ        copy.  A lot of people do that, get hooked on the game, and go out  บ
 บ        and buy it for themselves so they can play single player.  We also  บ
 บ        have some fairly innovative protection schemes to stop at least     บ
 บ        the casual hackers.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Such as?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : I have not seen a fully working crack, most of them are             บ
 บ        incomplete.  They don't work multi-player, you can't load save      บ
 บ        games, certain scenarios aren't in, etc.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Hybrid was first to release WarCraft 2.  However, their version     บ
 บ        was not fully operational.  It took them three days to get out a    บ
 บ        version with full network and scenario options.  In this time, do   บ
 บ        you think they were getting rid of the "innovative protection       บ
 บ        schemes?"                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Well, first off we need to clarify something here.  We realize we   บ
 บ        are never going to release an uncrackable game.  Our main goal is   บ
 บ        to stop the casual copiers.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I personal have not used the Hybrid crack, yet some people claim    บ
 บ        that it breaks up in Internet games or sometimes does not run at    บ
 บ        all.  Could this be intent or merely coincidence?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : It's our intent, I have yet to see a fully 100% crack of a cracked  บ
 บ        copy of the game.  I've seen a 97.98%, maybe 99% functioning,       บ
 บ        however, there are so many places in the code that would have to    บ
 บ        be altered that it would probably only become with it to those      บ
 บ        people that feel they're on a mission from God to crack games.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Recently, id Software's Quake Beta 3 was released by ROR (Release   บ
 บ        on Rampage).  They claim to have members who are part of id         บ
 บ        Software.  This version of Quake had included nearly everything     บ
 บ        but id Software has yet to release it in stores.  Does Blizzard     บ
 บ        have problems with such leeks?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Well, as I understand it, ROR claims they released the full         บ
 บ        version of Quake but it really only a beta-stage testing version    บ
 บ        of Quake.  There are still a lot of bugs and there is no network    บ
 บ        play.  When we were doing WarCraft 2, a pre-release (magazine       บ
 บ        only) alpha was leaked to the Internet, and was all over the place  บ
 บ        very quickly.  Since then, we've serialized all our alphas and      บ
 บ        betas we have sent out and haven't had any similar problems.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The beta release of WarCraft 2 was all over the Internet very       บ
 บ        quickly, and is nothing like the final version.  What is            บ
 บ        Blizzard's feelings on the WarCraft 2 beta or unfinished products   บ
 บ        in general.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Well, the alpha release (a beta release is something released for   บ
 บ        actual testing, the alpha release was just to show off the game to  บ
 บ        some magazines) was very incomplete and didn't give a very good     บ
 บ        picture of the game at all.  Our main problem with them is that     บ
 บ        people will get them, and get erroneous messages 50 to 90% of the   บ
 บ        time.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If and when Diablo and StarCraft hits the pirate scene, is          บ
 บ        Blizzard going to do anything to prevent it?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : We're never going to be able to completely prevent piracy.          บ
 บ        However we can stem the tide, and make it so it's actually easier   บ
 บ        to buy the game than it is to go threw all the hassle of pirating   บ
 บ        it.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A new addition to Blizzard games "Battle.Net" will be implemented   บ
 บ        in upcoming releases such as Diablo and StarCraft.  What is         บ
 บ        "Battle.Net" going to have to protect from piracy?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Not all of that has been finalized, and some of it can't be         บ
 บ        released to the public.  But, it will be transparent to legitimate  บ
 บ        users.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When is Diablo planned for release?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : Diablo will be out some time this summer.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Thank you for your time and I hope to see more releases from        บ
 บ        Blizzard in the future.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BLZ : You will.  Thank you.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RTS : Well ever since summer hit, RTS hasn't been doing much.  Soon       บ
 บ        after the work of the council and I start our re-organizing we      บ
 บ        will be back in action.  RTS is a great group, with a great         บ
 บ        Leader.  RTS is getting a few more sites up and more bbses soon.    บ
 บ        We have lots coming to us.                                          บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : RATM                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Babysitting Damage...     Affiliation : Damage President     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When and how did the courier group known as Damage start up?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, it began after the leaders of Digital and the majority of     บ
 บ        the seniors decided to become part of GODS (Guild of                บ
 บ        Distributors).  Shingen and I were invited to become GODS members,  บ
 บ        but elected to stay behind, because we didn't want to leave 30 to   บ
 บ        50 Digital guys hanging.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is the status of Damage at this moment?  I was told that all   บ
 บ        the good couriers from Digital left to join GODS, so Damage is a    บ
 บ        courier group that doesn't have any good couriers, and thus,        บ
 บ        cannot really compete, is that true?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, all of the "big name" guys left but we still have             บ
 บ        hardworkers that felt they were left out of Digital's operations.   บ
 บ        We have excellent couriers, some who were brought in from           บ
 บ        elsewhere, and some that have turned over a new leaf with Digital.  บ
 บ        I would like to congratulate the crew for holding together now in   บ
 บ        this time of limbo while we acquire new sites, especially my        บ
 บ        council, Reap, Gatekeeper, Stranger, etc.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you mean when you say "some that have turned over a new     บ
 บ        leaf with Digital?"                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, others didn't do much because they weren't motivated, they    บ
 บ        didn't like the leadership, or they didn't get accounts on sites    บ
 บ        or whatever.  They recognized the new leadership and were willing   บ
 บ        to become active again and give the new leadership a chance.  I     บ
 บ        think it's working out well.  Shingen, Damage Vice-President, has   บ
 บ        also been working very hard, keeping things together, and           บ
 บ        recruiting us new sites.  I like the positive attitude shown by     บ
 บ        everyone in the group, and with a little more time and patience we  บ
 บ        can become one of the better courier teams on the scene.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You are also the RCN senior member in charge of the RCN www, has    บ
 บ        becoming the President of Damage hurt your status in RCN since you  บ
 บ        seem to be neglecting your RCN duties (hint, hint)?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, no, I am working on an update to the RCN www, which           บ
 บ        currently resides on my HD.  I have been working 70 hours a week,   บ
 บ        and trying to manage Damage.  I've been doing all that while        บ
 บ        trying to maintain adequate sleep and a social life.  When you see  บ
 บ        the new RCN www, you will agree that I think I am balancing them    บ
 บ        all quite nicely.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Grin :)                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : GRIN =))                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You are suddenly the President of Damage, a respectable courier     บ
 บ        group, has that changed your status in the scene?  How did you      บ
 บ        come to that position, and what were your previous leadership       บ
 บ        experiences?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, Silent Mobius and Devast decided to give the group to         บ
 บ        Shingen and me, and Shingen in no way wanted to be the leader, so   บ
 บ        I assumed the role.  As for leadership experiences, I have none     บ
 บ        running a group on the Internet, but I have much experience         บ
 บ        coordinating and running things in real life, so I believe I have   บ
 บ        the raw skills necessary to do the job, they just need to be        บ
 บ        molded a bit for leadership on the Internet.  I work best under     บ
 บ        pressure, so I like that type of environment of trying to recover   บ
 บ        a group build character.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, you are more than capable of organizing many things,           บ
 บ        especially RCN things.  You seem to be quite good at that.          บ
 บ        Anyway, which ftp sites are part of Damage?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, as far as ftp sites go, I'm not at liberty to say, but I can  บ
 บ        tell you we are acquiring ftp sites at the rate of about one per    บ
 บ        week.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : These are private sites right?  I'm not talking about fake anon     บ
 บ        sites.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Correct, we don't deal in ANON sites, they are lame, and a great    บ
 บ        way to get busted.  I recommend ANON sites for those who want to    บ
 บ        fuck up the rest of their lives.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are you aware that when Digital split up to join GODS (now known    บ
 บ        as Amnesia), Damage was created and referred to as GODS' little     บ
 บ        brother group?  And that members of GODS were told to be nice to    บ
 บ        Damage couriers, and to perhaps babysit after Damage couriers?      บ
 บ        Don't you feel that the above statement limits the courier status   บ
 บ        and abilities of Damage to being second rate at best?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : I was and am fully aware of that.  It wasn't a FULL big brother     บ
 บ        thing, it was more of a pseudo big brother thing, I guess that's    บ
 บ        what you can call it.  The old Digital guys that left still wanted  บ
 บ        to remain faithful to Damage, and to help us with releases, a site  บ
 บ        or two, etc.  It wasn't a GODS thing, it was more of a former       บ
 บ        Digital member thing.  I think we need it to get back on our feet,  บ
 บ        and once we become self sufficient, we'll ask and need less and     บ
 บ        less help.  I feel this nurtures our ablilites, enabling us to      บ
 บ        grow and become good couriers and respected couriers.  I don't see  บ
 บ        us as their baby group, or something like that.  We are all         บ
 บ        friends from Digital, and we intend to remain that way.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did you just say "releases?"  Damage releases too?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Releases, meaning released stuff, getting it to Damage so we have   บ
 บ        more to spread so we can get credits to get more files, etc.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are your feelings on the fact that Digital split up to merge   บ
 บ        into GODS, only to see that GODS died, and then later renamed       บ
 บ        itself to Amnesia?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, it's sort of ironic that they are now named a group that we   บ
 บ        onced competed against, but its not the same Amnesia.  Key GODS     บ
 บ        members such as Quazimodem left the group, so none of the original  บ
 บ        GODS members remained.  So they felt it was stupid to remain as     บ
 บ        GODS.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Perhaps GODS died because you weren't a part of it?  They seem to   บ
 บ        need someone who can orgazine the group.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DMG : Well, not to say that I could've prevented it, but I believe        บ
 บ        contributions from Shingen and I may have helped the group get      บ
 บ        along better, but the past is the past and I yam where I yam, as    บ
 บ        Popeye would say.                                                   บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Zima Man             บ
 บ    Subject  : MTY Dupes PNC!?           Affiliation : Pinnacle Senior      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A few months ago, Pinnacle was heralded by Jimmy Jamez, the         บ
 บ        President of DOD (Drink or Die), as the #3 utils group in the       บ
 บ        scene, do you believe that is still true at the present time?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : No, I do not believe that is true at the moment.  Pinnacle is not   บ
 บ        currently #3 in the utils scene, but I believe that we are either   บ
 บ        #4 or #5 depending on how you look at it.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why do you believe that Pinnacle is no longer the #3 utils group    บ
 บ        in the scene, if that is so, then which group has taken its place?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Well we had some internal problems in the group and the group has   บ
 บ        declined in its releasing power.  As time passed we began slacking  บ
 บ        off and practically became dead.  In my opinion the #3 utils group  บ
 บ        right now is Mortality.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I was recently informed that Mortality, a well respected utils      บ
 บ        group, duped Pinnacle on 3 releases in a short week, is that true?  บ
 บ        If so, what happened?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : A month ago, a guy applied to Pinnacle as a supplier and I told     บ
 บ        him to show me some releases.  Some time passed and he offered      บ
 บ        Xref, Netpak Proffesional, and Internet ToolPak, which are Visual   บ
 บ        Basic tools by a company called Crescent, for Pinnacle.  I told     บ
 บ        him that Pinnacle already released Xref and Netpak Professional, I  บ
 บ        was the one who supplied it so I knew it better then anyone, and I  บ
 บ        also told him that Internet Toolpak v1.0 was released by Pinnacle   บ
 บ        and and that v2.0 was released by some small group just a week      บ
 บ        before he offered it to me.  Apparently, the supplier thought I     บ
 บ        was bullshiting and since I told him that Pinnacle is not           บ
 บ        interested in these releases he decided to goto Mortality.  I have  บ
 บ        all products done by Crescent and I released most of them with the  บ
 บ        exception of a few.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you believe that the supplier told Mortality that Pinnacle was   บ
 บ        not interested because Pinnacle believed that those releases were   บ
 บ        dupes?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : I guess Mortality was busy that week and didn't do a good job dupe  บ
 บ        checking it.  He also released a Visual Basic tool called Enquiry   บ
 บ        which he claimed to be 1 disk when in reality it's 3 disks and I    บ
 บ        have it and I will release it when I fix my HD.  Mortality is a     บ
 บ        kick ass group and I was very dissapointed to see them dupe and     บ
 บ        release a broken copy of Enquiry.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned earlier that there were some internal problems in     บ
 บ        Pinnacle that almost caused its death, what were these problems?    บ
 บ        And what brought it back up after it almost died?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Well, 2 of the seniors were really sick and spent a lot of time in  บ
 บ        the hospital and Iron Steel had some family problems.  Back in      บ
 บ        October of 1995, we also lost one of our founders, Bishop, who      บ
 บ        went to PWA (Pirates with Attitudes) and our best suppliers said    บ
 บ        farewell to the funky business of releasing.  Since the end of      บ
 บ        November of 1995, we started to release less and less and we had    บ
 บ        on average 4 releases per week and by January of 1996 we became     บ
 บ        idle.  In my opinion, Pinnacle was never dead, we just took a       บ
 บ        break so I kept it alive and we are back in business again.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What role did you play in the creation of Pinnacle?  Your role as   บ
 บ        the current leader of Pinnacle is undisputed, but how did you       บ
 บ        become its leader?  Were you also one of the original founders of   บ
 บ        Pinnacle?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Believe it or not, I was not one of the founders of Pinnacle.  My   บ
 บ        career in Pinnacle began in October of 1995 when I got the          บ
 บ        position as the member coordinator.  From there, I rose up to what  บ
 บ        I am today.  The original founders of Pinnacle were Count Zero,     บ
 บ        Blazen, and Bishop.  Bishop is currently with PWA, Count Zero with  บ
 บ        a small group called Dark*Star, and Blazen has moved to AOL.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did Bishop leave Pinnacle for PWA?  PWA is a much larger group  บ
 บ        and is considered the #1 utils group in the scene, but that should  บ
 บ        be no reason why Bishop would want to leave the group he was a      บ
 บ        founder of, to join another group he was unfamiliar with?  Did he   บ
 บ        have no loyalty towards the group he helped create?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : I have no clue why he abandoned us because he left a few days       บ
 บ        before I joined Pinnacle.  I don't think that he wasn't loyal, he   บ
 บ        had his own reasons to leave.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How does Pinnacle get its releases?  Do most Pinnacle suppliers do  บ
 บ        store pick up, or are there Pinnacle suppliers that have            บ
 บ        connections within companies?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : All of us do it differently.  Some work in stores, some work in     บ
 บ        places that buy software, but only a few have actual company        บ
 บ        contacts.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : At one point in time, Pinnacle was a utils only group, but          บ
 บ        recently, I have to say that I am surprised or sad to see that      บ
 บ        Pinnacle has released a few games, why is that so?  Pinnacle is a   บ
 บ        quality utils group and some must wonder why it is starting to      บ
 บ        release games.  Has Pinnacle's quality of standard dropped in the   บ
 บ        recent months?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Actually we have released games almost since the birth of the       บ
 บ        group but not that many.  When our suppliers had games and we       บ
 บ        didn't have enough time to trade the game we released them.  But    บ
 บ        it didn't happen a lot and we released only a few good              บ
 บ        games/addons but as of last month, Pinnacle is utils only.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many releases would you say Pinnacle releases each week         บ
 บ        nowadays?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : I would have to say about 5 releases a week if you count all the    บ
 บ        things we released in the last month.  Last week and this week, we  บ
 บ        are doing very poorly because me and one more supplier are having   บ
 บ        hardware problems and are unable to release anything.  I usually    บ
 บ        download the release before releasing it and test it and I am       บ
 บ        unable to do it since I get CRC errors in every fucking zip I       บ
 บ        download as well as for every zip I zip myself.  So when my HD      บ
 บ        gets fixed (hopefully this weekend) then you will see a lot more    บ
 บ        releases from us.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Perhaps you have a virus?  Many people do complain that some        บ
 บ        Pinnacle releases do not work, what do you have to say to people    บ
 บ        that complain about Pinnacle's broken releases?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : I don't have a virus I just have to change the mode of my HD to     บ
 บ        LBA and format it.  Can you tell me specifically which releases     บ
 บ        were claimed as broken?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : People have come up to me claiming that your 19 disk release of     บ
 บ        Land Designer 3D v4.0 are missing some files and won't even         บ
 บ        install.  Is that true?  I personally would have no need for        บ
 บ        landscaping software, nor would I download copyrighted material.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Yes, that is absolutely true and I want to apologize to all those   บ
 บ        people who spent time downloading it.  The problem with this        บ
 บ        release was that the supplier didn't know how to rip it and test    บ
 บ        it and I had to help him.  He did a good job ripping it and         บ
 บ        testing it but he forget to take out the original cd out of his cd  บ
 บ        drive and he had no problems installing it from HD.  It was his     บ
 บ        first rip and he made a mistake and everyone makes mistakes once    บ
 บ        in a while.  Other than that there were no broken releases.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, we all make mistakes, and it's what we do after we make the    บ
 บ        mistakes that separates the good from the bad.  Was a fix or a      บ
 บ        fixed version of the program ever released by Pinnacle?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : No, at least not yet. The guy who supplied it asked the legendary   บ
 บ        Misha to do a crack for him but I don't know what's going on with   บ
 บ        it.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : But it's been almost a week since it was originally released?       บ
 บ        Wouldn't another utils group jump on that release by now?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : Yes and he asked him right after we found out that its broken.      บ
 บ        That just shows that not every group is capable of getting some     บ
 บ        stuff that we get while others are.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You said earlier that Pinnacle released about 5 releases each       บ
 บ        week, that is a very impressive number, but does that number        บ
 บ        include releases such PPEs which are freeware mods for PCBoard?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : No, we haven't released PPEs in a long time.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you see happening to Pinnacle in the future?  Do you see    บ
 บ        it becoming the pinnacle of utils release groups, or do you         บ
 บ        believe that it would once again reach a low point and even         บ
 บ        perhaps die off?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  PNC : I don't think Pinnacle will die, at least not as long as I'm in     บ
 บ        it.  Time will only show what will happen to us but I believe we    บ
 บ        will become stronger.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Kang                 บ
 บ    Subject  : Couriers Releasing?       Affiliation : THC Senior           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Could you start by telling me your current affiliations.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : My main affiliation is THC (The Hardened Criminals) right now.  I   บ
 บ        am involved with other groups, but I'm not as dedicated with other  บ
 บ        groups as I am with THC.  I am really trying to focus on THC        บ
 บ        because of all the new changes that have been implemented.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are these changes within THC that would require your           บ
 บ        attention?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : For those who don't already know, THC has moved to becoming a       บ
 บ        release group, we used to courier and release, but we only release  บ
 บ        now.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A courier group has gone to release?  How did all this happen?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : Well, we have dropped a lot of couriers and idlers.  The old        บ
 บ        couriers were moved to other big courier groups like fATE (Fast     บ
 บ        Action Trade Exchange), Motiv8, and RiSC (Rise in Superior          บ
 บ        Couriering).  The slow couriers that weren't doing anything were    บ
 บ        just cut.  BBS couriers were kept because we will still need them.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I know fATE, Motiv8, and RiSC well enough to know that they just    บ
 บ        don't accept any couriers, you have to be good.  How did you guys   บ
 บ        get them in there?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : Well, remember we only sent over the good couriers.  Super Hacker   บ
 บ        knows some people in there, and setup some deals with them.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So by dropping a few couriers, THC moved over from couriering to    บ
 บ        releasing?  That couldn't have been the only step, what else was    บ
 บ        involved in the transition?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : Oh no.  We have also added some suppliers, and are making projects  บ
 บ        to raise some money for THC, and therefore get some releases.  We   บ
 บ        have also been talking with people that work for some big           บ
 บ        companies to also supply for us.                                    บ

 บ        games group, a utils group, or will THC be releasing both games     บ
 บ        and utils?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THC : We are releasing both.  I know it may sound like a bad idea, but    บ
 บ        we can easily get the job done and kick a lot of other release      บ
 บ        groups asses!  We've already released several builds of NT and we   บ
 บ        are good at getting software that's by Microsoft.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        that are already well established?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        been a release group for about 2 days and already have had          บ
 บ        working, fully cracked releases.  That already puts THC above       บ
 บ        other groups that can't crack, groups like.. Napalm.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        our official couriers and boards.                                   บ

 บ        official courier group for THC, or is there none?                   บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <LostSoul> You promised me that it was for personal use, don't lie to     บ
 บ             me.  You tricked me.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Prophet> Yes, I know I said that, but I didn't know you would mind that  บ
 บ            I use it.  I'm very sorry for this man.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You might be confused as to what the above log meant.  According to   บ
 บ  Lost Soul, Prophet came up to him to have a game cracked.  At first,      บ
 บ  Lost Soul was not willing to crack the game for Prophet because Prophet   บ
 บ  could have released the crack for a game for Napalm.  Lost Soul is a      บ
 บ  Prestige cracker and is thus, not allowed to crack games for other games  บ
 บ  groups such as Napalm.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Prophet then saw that he had no choice but to lie to Lost Soul.       บ
 บ  Prophet said that the game Lost Soul would be cracking would not be used  บ
 บ  in a release by Napalm, but was merely for his own personal use.          บ
 บ  Innocently, Lost Soul agrees and cracks the game for Prophet, only to     บ
 บ  find that his crack was later released by Napalm.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Napalm couldn't get a game cracked, so they had to trick an innocent  บ
 บ  Prestige cracker into cracking it for them.  Since Napalm doesn't seem    บ
 บ  to have any crackers, and none seem to want to join Napalm, if you do     บ
 บ  happen to be a cracker, beware, don't be surprised if Prophet comes up    บ
 บ  to you and tries to trick you in the same manner he tricked Lost Soul.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Subject : Coredump... Literally?                                        บ

 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ      Coredump is a new group run by Incarnate.  Generally new groups       บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Oxygen                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : Don't Type.. TALK!!!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The past few days, I've been reflecting on something.  New            บ
 บ  communications packages and breakthroughs are popping up, and in my       บ
 บ  opinion, can be used to our advantage.  By using voice technology and     บ
 บ  new file transfer tools, the warez scene as we know it can take a big     บ
 บ  leap as far as trading is concerned, and provide both group and trader    บ
 บ  to trader interaction with a new, exciting, and easy to use medium.  Two  บ
 บ  programs that I have tried and feel meet these requirements are Internet  บ
 บ  Phone Release 4, by VocalTec and Internet Party Line by Intel.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Internet Phone Release 4 is a valuable tool.  It provides several     บ
 บ  features, with an easy to learn interface.  Hidden under all the pretty   บ
 บ  cartoons and modern buttons, lies a great multimedia communications       บ
 บ  package, just waiting to be used.  Over the past few days, I've been      บ
 บ  using the software, trying out the different tools such as file           บ
 บ  transfers (zip, txt, jpg, you name it), the whiteboard, text chat, voice  บ
 บ  mail and of course the main focus of the program, voice capabilities.     บ
 บ  Iphone4 lets users create their own channels, and allows other people     บ
 บ  who have the same interests to easily find and join these channels.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Some channels that would probably be of interest to the average       บ
 บ  elite are Warez, Warez Sites, #Warez666, and even RCN has a channel open  บ
 บ  for people to gather, named RCN of course, and new channels pop up        บ
 บ  daily.  Through the RCN channel, myself, RoadRebel, and a few others      บ
 บ  have gotten together and found out it can be both fun, and valuable to    บ
 บ  utilize Iphone to conduct small private meetings.  I can show Road Rebel  บ
 บ  an article I am working on, and talk about it on the spot, we can         บ
 บ  transfer files easily, and many other features make it just a great       บ
 บ  tool.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Internet Party Line lets more then one person get together to have    บ
 บ  voice meetings.  Also available is a text chat window, for people who     บ
 บ  need it.  What the program lacks in interface it makes up for in how it   บ
 บ  brings several people together for one purpose.  Groups can use this to   บ
 บ  conduct their meetings in a new way, or they can use it just to chat      บ
 บ  with friends.  I think Internet Party Line is decent, but it pales in     บ
 บ  comparison to the Internet Phone.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I hope this gives you some insight on how you can use these tools to  บ
 บ  help bring your group together, transfer files, talk, and show each       บ
 บ  other information on Iphone's whiteboard, and basically have fun.  And    บ
 บ  if you ever need help, I'm Oxygen in the Internet Phone Directory, look   บ
 บ  for me in RCN, see ya!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿       ฿฿
