 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Gorilla                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Old vs. New or My Time Was Better than Yours                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is a comment spurred by Hitex/RC's reply to Bollox in RCN-19.    บ
 บ  Bollox stated "how severely messed up the scene is today" and H/RC        บ
 บ  replied "... I won't believe it that the scene was ever any better. ...   บ
 บ  couldn't have been too excited when you downloaded Pong... "              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am a long time trader, well known locally to any long-time pirate   บ
 บ  in 516.  I have been BBSing and moving files for over 12 yrs.  I started  บ
 บ  with the Commie, went to a TI 99/4A followed by the TI Professional, and  บ
 บ  then various IBM clones. I have been, and no doubt will again, be a BBS   บ
 บ  sysop running Telegard, Celerity, and PCB.  I have been IRCing for less   บ
 บ  than a year now.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Let me assure H/RC I was THRILLED when I got my first C64 program     บ
 บ  off of The Gull many years ago.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Everyone suffers from the "my time was better than yours" syndrome.   บ
 บ  Ask your parents and their parents.  Everyone feels their time was the    บ
 บ  best.  The great thing about memories is that they are changeable by the  บ
 บ  one remembering them.  As time passes, that which sucked when we were     บ
 บ  young either becomes a positive or fades from active recollection.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So the concept that at any one time, and the scene encompassed by     บ
 บ  it, is any "better" than another is a waste of effort.  It is             บ
 บ  comparisons that matter not hard truths.  The scene not all that long     บ
 บ  ago (since I'm 41 it doesn't seem long) was quite different.  That's      บ
 บ  about all you can say about it.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When I started "elite" meant just that; you had to know someone who   บ
 บ  knew someone who knew someone to even get a BBS number to call for        บ
 บ  files.  As a sysop, I had tons of new members who would call my BBS and   บ
 บ  seem to be under the impression that they were "elite" simply because     บ
 บ  they had a modem and enough sense (and even that wasn't always true) to   บ
 บ  use it.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Their qualifications for accessing my BBS and their definition of     บ
 บ  "eleet" (and how I DO hate this butchering of the English Language) did   บ
 บ  not in any sense compare with mine.  My definition was longevity,         บ
 บ  computer knowledge, innate intelligence, their reputation, desire,        บ
 บ  politeness and contacts, i.e. who do you know that I know?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Theirs was "I am on IRC and get 0-day warez."  Theirs was "I'm in     บ
 บ  XXX."  Theirs was "I'm kewL."  Theirs was "I've been trading for 2        บ
 บ  months and my bud, who vouches for me has been in the scene almost a      บ
 บ  month longer!"  Theirs was "Hey, you need me more Fo0L than I need you."  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As far as being on IRC goes, so what?  Is like IRC selective or       บ
 บ  something?  All you need is a channel name, a 2kps or better connection   บ
 บ  and don't prove yourself to be a TOTAL asshole and you can get all the    บ
 บ  0-day you want.  It's not hard and it tells me nothing about "you."       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And your warez group, so what?  Many (if not most) of these groups    บ
 บ  suck.  It used to be if you got a file, it would work cause the group     บ
 บ  had a rep to maintain.  Now, groups & their members come and go like      บ
 บ  farts in the wind.  Pride and personal reputation is a rapidly vanishing  บ
 บ  concept.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You're "kewL?"  What do you mean by that?  You do drugs? Hell, a      บ
 บ  pussy from 1972 did more drugs in a week than you'll do in a lifetime.    บ
 บ  You mean you get files?  What files?  Useful working ones?  You're        บ
 บ  "kewL" because you know what all those group initials mean?  So does      บ
 บ  anyone who can download a text file.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You've been in the scene 2 months?  Wow!  And your friend has been    บ
 บ  in 3????  I'm impressed!                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And "I need you more than you need me?"  Even if true (and it never   บ
 บ  has been), that isn't a very smart thing to say to me, is it?  At best,   บ
 บ  it is rude.  Your momma may still be wiping your ass when you take a      บ
 บ  shit but don't expect me to.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Internet has made things more democratic which is good.  I am     บ
 บ  elite but I never wanted to be an elitist.  But, like all changes, that   บ
 บ  silver cloud comes complete with a dark lining.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BBSing "way back when" was not solely about files.  Files were small  บ
 บ  so it left you enough time to leech and still do other stuff.  BBSing     บ
 บ  was about "community."  It was a shared secret.  A BBS was a place were   บ
 บ  people could communicate with others who shared that secret.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With the size of files nowadays, and the spread of those huge files   บ
 บ  over the Internet, who "talks" anymore?  How much talk goes on in the     บ
 บ  channels and if there is any, how much of it is even worth reading?       บ
 บ  And, assuming you BBS, how many elite boards even get any quality posts   บ
 บ  any more?                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The death of BBSing (and I personally doubt it will ever die unlike   บ
 บ  some) can be traced to large files and the "impersonality" of the         บ
 บ  Internet, where a person "surfs" but never gets wet.  They do not, and    บ
 บ  can not, immerse themselves in what was, at one time, more than a hobby,  บ
 บ  it was an avocation.  You BELIEVED in it.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Who believes in anything any more?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So let's not compare "my" days in the scene with "yours."  I made     บ
 บ  friends, you know nicks.  Your files are often much better but mine had   บ
 บ  "playability."  Your files are easier to get but mine always worked.      บ
 บ  You get stuff faster, but my stuff stayed around longer.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, be happy with what you have.  If you stay in the scene for more   บ
 บ  than a year or two, the new kids coming up are going to consider you a    บ
 บ  dinosaur too.  They will argue and laugh at you when you are tempted in   บ
 บ  years to come to tell them, "Things were better when I first got into     บ
 บ  the scene."                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ    Author  : Karen                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Being Female in a Male Internet                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What's life like on the Internet for a female?  Well, I'll attempt    บ
 บ  to fill you in on the little things that will probably make many of you   บ
 บ  go "Hmm".                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I started out on the Internet many, many moons ago.  I had a          บ
 บ  particular friend who was into BBS'ing as much as me at the time, who     บ
 บ  wanted to show me this thing called the Internet.  "How much better than  บ
 บ  BBS'ing can it be?" I asked myself.  Well, I don't think I've even come   บ
 บ  close to being as elated as I was that day.  What I saw was his hard      บ
 บ  drive overflowing with warez.  Immediatley, I wanted to have a piece of   บ
 บ  it - I needed it - it needed me.  I was hooked by the time I walked out   บ
 บ  his door and drove home.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Later that day, I had my own Internet account.  My own account on     บ
 บ  the Internet!  Wow, this was really cool!  OK, time to start doing what   บ
 บ  many of us do best.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      CLANG!                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Wait a minute.  All these people on here are males!  "What!? You      บ
 บ  don't believe I'm female?! Aww, come on give me a break!"  Needless to    บ
 บ  say, I found it very difficult on the Internet at first until I started   บ
 บ  making some friends.  Having a female nick on IRC can have it's           บ
 บ  disadvantages, but I decided to stay with it - come what may.  I guess    บ
 บ  being female has it's advantages too, as I started to meet some pretty    บ
 บ  influential people within the warez scene.  Within a few months I had     บ
 บ  become a respected Op on many of the #WarezX channels, and started to     บ
 บ  have an influence on what happened within the politics of each.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      About two years after my introduction to the Internet, I decided to   บ
 บ  get a permanent connection.  I was a true Net-head(ess).  I would leave   บ
 บ  all of my sessions running, even IRC.  I remember coming home from work   บ
 บ  to find 30+ messages per day asking for Netsex and the like.  Daily, I    บ
 บ  would get mass invited to many #Sex type channels, and quickly realized   บ
 บ  that I needed to learn as much as possible about revenge on IRC.  Enter   บ
 บ  my experience with Killer Gold (An mIRC script) which gave me the         บ
 บ  ammunition that I needed to combat the day-to-day nasties that I          บ
 บ  encountered.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I now work with a mojor ISP in Australia, which allows me privileges  บ
 บ  that I would not normally get as a mere user (plus my permanent           บ
 บ  connection is free now!).  I get to chat with the administrators of       บ
 บ  other ISPs, and request that any users that give me an exeptionally hard  บ
 บ  time have their accounts revoked, etc.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I live on the Internet and like anyone else, I can see most bad       บ
 บ  situations before they approach me.  Experience counts for everything.    บ
 บ  When the situation warrants it, I call in the services of my friends.     บ
 บ  They've always been there for me since the start, and they will always    บ
 บ  be there.  They are true friends. We all have true friends, and we all    บ
 บ  know who they are.  I thank all my true friends.  I would do anything     บ
 บ  for them in return.  Life deals us many hands, and we have to learn how   บ
 บ  to react.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Being a female in a male dominated area is hard to get used to at     บ
 บ  first, but when you meet the right people, it just clicks.  We are all    บ
 บ  friends.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Software Piracy Association                                   บ
 บ    Subject : Protecting Software in a CD-Recordable World                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is an excerpt from the SPA's information file           บ
 บ  concerning their stance on software piracy and what they intend to do to  บ
 บ  prevent piracy :                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The Threat                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Piracy has been a major problem in the diskette-based software        บ
 บ  market since the introduction of commercial software.  SPA (Software      บ
 บ  Piracy Association) did not collect piracy figures for the total          บ
 บ  software industry until 1993, due to a lack of data on the extent of      บ
 บ  consumer piracy.  However, a glance at the data for business              บ
 บ  applications tells the conservative story.  In 1989, the total business   บ
 บ  applications market in the U.S. was $3.1 billion, with a 48% piracy rate  บ
 บ  which is equal to $2.3 billion in lost revenues for software publishers.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By 1994, the piracy rate in the U.S. market had dropped to 25%, or    บ
 บ  $1.05 billion in losses for the $4.2 billion market.  The consumer        บ
 บ  market reached $1.3 billion that year.  While we do not know the true     บ
 บ  size of consumer piracy, we can safely assume that it constitutes a       บ
 บ  large and expanding portion of the total software industry losses.  In    บ
 บ  the SPA's 1995 Consumer Survey, 20% of respondents admitted to openly     บ
 บ  copying software.  While the piracy rate in the U.S. has steadily         บ
 บ  declined since 1989, in international markets piracy has increasingly     บ
 บ  become a vexing problem.  In 1994, SPA estimated that the piracy rate     บ
 บ  internationally was 49%.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      While CD-ROM software has, until now, been relatively protected from  บ
 บ  the threat of end-user piracy by the expense of CD-recordable             บ
 บ  technology, the threat to software publishers is threefold :              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) As the cost of CD recorders (CD-Rs) rapidly decreases, the        บ
 บ          threat of CD-ROM piracy among end-users dramatically increases.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) The software market which is now an international market, faces   บ
 บ          jurisdictional differences, wherein pirated software is           บ
 บ          considered low priority.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Counterfeit software from offshore is being shipped into the      บ
 บ          U.S. for rapid sale.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In light of this increased threat to CD-ROM software, SPA has begun   บ
 บ  an investigation into potential solutions. Potential solutions cover the  บ
 บ  range from software and hardware solutions, to legal and legislative      บ
 บ  remedies.  What follows is a critical assessment of all available         บ
 บ  options.  The goal of this report is to identify the option that          บ
 บ  maximizes protection from unauthorized duplication, while retaining the   บ
 บ  autonomy of each software publisher.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Potential Solutions                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By using complex algorithms, software applications can be encoded to  บ
 บ  ensure protection.  Encryption is primarily used to protect data that is  บ
 บ  being transferred via electronic distribution and on-line services.       บ
 บ  Encryption can also be used to protect software applications.             บ
 บ  Publishers could encrypt their software applications thereby making it    บ
 บ  impossible for an end-user to use a copy of the application unless they   บ
 บ  have the software 'key' to decrypt the software code and turn it into a   บ
 บ  usable format.  The end-user would be required to register the product    บ
 บ  (either on-line or through a 1-800 number), in order to decrypt the       บ
 บ  software. It is possible to create a unique encryption key for each       บ
 บ  end-user. Additionally, if a publisher is opposed to forced               บ
 บ  registration, encryption keys can be shipped with software applications.  บ
 บ  However, by shipping encryption keys you allow the end-user to make a     บ
 บ  copy of the application and the key.  Encryption has great potential      บ
 บ  because it can protect software that is being transmitted via electronic  บ
 บ  distribution methods as well as CD-ROMs.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Protection built into the software application itself.  Software can  บ
 บ  be configured in a variety of ways in order to ensure protection.         บ
 บ  Software protection can be configured to restrict the number of           บ
 บ  executions prior to registration, allow only network installation or      บ
 บ  single PC installation, and to restrict the amount of time in which an    บ
 บ  application can be used prior to registration.  Software applications     บ
 บ  can be configured, once installation is complete to take a footprint of   บ
 บ  the resident hard drive.  Once a footprint has been taken, the software   บ
 บ  application can only be used in conjunction with that hard drive, this    บ
 บ  prevents users from making additional copies and passing them along to    บ
 บ  friends.  Depending upon the type of software protection used, an         บ
 บ  on-line or 1-800 registration may have to be set up by the publisher for  บ
 บ  authorized users.  Software protection also allows for distribution       บ
 บ  across multiple media.  The benefit to the software publisher would be    บ
 บ  that the same form of software protection could be used for CD-ROMS,      บ
 บ  diskettes, and for electronic distribution.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Dongles are hardware keys which allow applications to be run on       บ
 บ  personal computers and file servers.  Dongles are a separate piece of     บ
 บ  hardware that can either be provided with the product or purchased        บ
 บ  separately.  Software must be configured to ensure that it cannot be run  บ
 บ  without the appropriate dongle.  Publishers that select this option will  บ
 บ  probably need to manufacture several different dongles.  Most likely      บ
 บ  there would have to be a dongle for each version of the software and      บ
 บ  different configurations (PC and network).  On-line and electronic        บ
 บ  distribution of software applications is possible with dongles, but both  บ
 บ  the software application and the dongle itself are required for the user  บ
 บ  to execute the application.  Currently, dongles are used for high end     บ
 บ  vertical applications as well as high cost applications such as CAD       บ
 บ  software applications.  One of the major drawbacks to this option is      บ
 บ  cost.  The cost of a single dongle (approximately $30) can conceivably    บ
 บ  double the cost of a consumer application.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Software protection can be used as an additional measure to protect   บ
 บ  software using encryption technology.  Decrypted applications can be      บ
 บ  configured in a variety of different ways through use of software         บ
 บ  protection in order to prevent unauthorized duplication.  Encryption's    บ
 บ  strength lies in its ability to protect software applications via         บ
 บ  electronic distribution while software protection is most successful in   บ
 บ  preventing end user piracy.  When used together, software protection and  บ
 บ  encryption provide the best line of defense against software piracy.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The motion picture and recording industries have faced similar        บ
 บ  threats as those posed by CD-R technology to software publishers.  A      บ
 บ  review of the Betamax and DAT issues and their respective industry        บ
 บ  responses will be useful in the development of a software industry        บ
 บ  response to CD-Rs.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The issue of copyright infringement and electronic recording          บ
 บ  technology was first raised with the introduction of the Betamax VCR.     บ
 บ  Universal Studios and Walt Disney Productions sued Sony Corporation for   บ
 บ  contributory copyright infringement (Sony Corporation of America vs.      บ
 บ  Universal City Studios). Universal argued that "time-shifting " of        บ
 บ  copyrighted programs broadcast over television constituted copyright      บ
 บ  infringement and Sony, as producer of the technology that enabled         บ
 บ  "time-shifting" was a contributory infringer to any acts of this nature.  บ
 บ  In 1984, the Supreme Court ruled that non-commercial "time-shifting" of   บ
 บ  copyrighted programs does not impair the value of the copyrighted work,   บ
 บ  and therefore may be considered fair use.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The introduction of home digital audio recording products in the      บ
 บ  late 1980's raised the recording industry's interest in potential         บ
 บ  copyright infringement due to the ability of digital recorders to         บ
 บ  produce identical copies of sound recordings.  In 1987 the hardware for   บ
 บ  a digital audio tape (DAT) first became available in Japan and Europe.    บ
 บ  Electronics manufacturers and the recording industry each had an          บ
 บ  interest in resolving the issue prior to the introduction of DAT          บ
 บ  technology in the U.S.  The electronics industry feared the threat of     บ
 บ  vicarious copyright infringement lawsuits by record producers and         บ
 บ  composers and the recording industry had fought for a royalty scheme to   บ
 บ  benefit copyright producers from home audio taping since the              บ
 บ  introduction of audio cassette recorders in 1963.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In 1989, the International Recording Industry and the Consumer        บ
 บ  Electronics Industry reached a compromise during their meeting in         บ
 บ  Athens, Greece.  This agreement stipulated that manufacturers of DAT      บ
 บ  machines were to insert Serial Copy Management Systems (SCMS) into all    บ
 บ  consumer DAT recorders.  SCMS prevents users from making digital          บ
 บ  recordings of first generation copies, but allows unlimited copying from  บ
 บ  an original source recording.  In 1990, Samuel Cahn and four music        บ
 บ  publishing companies forestalled the implementation of this compromise    บ
 บ  by filing a class action infringement suit against Sony Corporation       บ
 บ  (Cahn vs. Sony) in an attempt to bar DAT technology from the United       บ
 บ  States.  This case was settled out of court in 1991.  The Sony-Cahn       บ
 บ  settlement was codified by Congress in the Audio Home Recording Act of    บ
 บ  1992 (AHRA).                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The AHRA has three significant provisions : 6                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) Mandatory implementation of SCMS or some similar serial copy      บ
 บ          protection on all digital audio recording equipment.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) Mandatory royalty scheme on recording media and equipment         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Prohibition of copyright infringement actions based on home       บ
 บ          copying                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      SCMS implementation has allayed many recording industry fears that    บ
 บ  unauthorized digital audio taping would become a cottage industry.        บ
 บ  Additionally, the implementation of a royalty scheme has allowed US       บ
 บ  producers to take advantage of reciprocity with international royalty     บ
 บ  programs.  While the SCMS implementation and royalty scheme have been     บ
 บ  beneficial to the recording industry, they also have drawbacks.  As       บ
 บ  mentioned earlier, SCMS does not prevent unauthorized copying from an     บ
 บ  original source, therefore as long as an original source is purchased by  บ
 บ  the consumer, the consumer is free to make copies from that source.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The royalty scheme developed under AHRA has been largely              บ
 บ  unsuccessful.  This is because the royalties are based upon a percentage  บ
 บ  value of the recording equipment and media.  Since 1992, the cost of      บ
 บ  these recorders and their media has dropped significantly.  As such,      บ
 บ  royalties are now only a fraction of what they were when the Act was      บ
 บ  passed.  The largest drawback of the AHRA is the provision prohibiting    บ
 บ  the filing of copyright infringement litigation action based on home      บ
 บ  copying.  This provision is essentially an erosion of the rights granted  บ
 บ  by the Copyright Act of 1976.  By including this provision, AHRA removes  บ
 บ  the question of whether home taping constitutes fair use by making home   บ
 บ  taping a non-infringing activity.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Recommendation                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The motion picture and sound recording industries have used           บ
 บ  litigation and legislation, respectively, to control new reproduction     บ
 บ  technologies, but these efforts have been either unsuccessful or          บ
 บ  unprofitable.  Rather than follow in their footsteps, SPA staff           บ
 บ  recommends that SPA members endorse the incorporation of encryption and   บ
 บ  software protection into titles and applications distributed in CD-ROM    บ
 บ  format, as the best means for SPA to fight software piracy by end-users   บ
 บ  and other "middle men" using CD-Rs.  SPA will seek legislation and        บ
 บ  regulatory changes in the US, Canada, and other countries that will make  บ
 บ  effective and reliable encryption available to software publishers.  SPA  บ
 บ  will also pursue legislation that will prohibit the manufacture and sale  บ
 บ  of devices or services intended primarily to defeat anti-copying          บ
 บ  technology.  By opting for the protection offered by encryption and       บ
 บ  software protection, publishers will retain their right to protect their  บ
 บ  software applications from unauthorized duplication and will not          บ
 บ  sacrifice any of the remedies available under the Copyright Act once      บ
 บ  infringement is discovered.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In order to facilitate discussion on this critical issue to SPA       บ
 บ  members, the SPA will host a round table discussion on the CD-R issue     บ
 บ  and encryption and software protection solutions for all SPA members at   บ
 บ  the Spring Symposium in San Francisco.  The purpose of this round table   บ
 บ  will be to bring together publishers and SPA members involved in the      บ
 บ  production of encryption and software protection technologies in order    บ
 บ  to give publishers the chance to express their needs to the developers    บ
 บ  that will supply this technology in the future.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Several SPA Member Companies (protection providers) participated in   บ
 บ  an interactive session with CD-ROM publishers at the Spring Symposium.    บ
 บ  The discussion focused on the types of technology available to help       บ
 บ  prevent duplication of CD-ROMs.  There are a wide variety of protections  บ
 บ  available depending upon the cost that the publisher is willing to        บ
 บ  undertake and the level of involvement that the publisher is willing to   บ
 บ  pass on to the end-user.  The take home message from this discussion, is  บ
 บ  that there will be no free lunch.  Technologies that are highly secure    บ
 บ  such as footprinting, hardware keys and encryption are high in cost and   บ
 บ  will increase the amount of steps an end-user will have to undertake      บ
 บ  before being able to use a product.  Lower level security products and    บ
 บ  techniques such as flash screen warnings and forced registrations will    บ
 บ  be low in cost, but will be easier to circumvent.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/12/96            ณ  บ

 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ

 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/30/96 -> 06/05/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/12/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ

 บ      Some of you have been wondering how do I manage to get all the games  บ
 บ  released each week and have time to play them and review them.  Well,     บ
 บ  it's simple!  I own this magic wand called the "Game-o-rizer."  What it   บ
 บ  does, is it magically downloads shit at 100 MB/S and then it              บ
 บ  automatically follows the directions in the NFOs and installs them, plays บ
 บ  them, and then writes about them.  See, I don't actually do anything,     บ
 บ  it's all my Game-o-rizer magic wand.  And now for a limited time only,    บ
 บ  you too can purchase a Game-o-rizer magic wand for the low price of only  บ
 บ  $1,999.  A steal at this low price, it comes in the following colors :    บ
 บ  Green, Red, Blue, White Cum, and Yellow Vaginal Yeast Infection.  To      บ
 บ  order, send chicks or babes to "Game-o-rizer," 11 Bullshit Dr., Smokey-   บ
 บ  Air, Los Angeles, California, 90210.  Shipping and handling only $50.     บ
 บ  Please allow 2-4 centuries for delivery, as it will be shipped through    บ
 บ  UPS.                                                                      บ

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Rating scale :                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ           (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                           บ
 บ          (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                     บ
 บ          (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                         บ
 บ          (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.     บ
 บ          (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.           บ
 บ          (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.       บ
 บ          (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                    บ
 บ              100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in 'ity.'  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow NFO directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just b/c it         บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ

 บ  Rise 2 Power explained the reason for their non-working release of Grand  บ
 บ  Pris 2, in one of their other releases.  Here it is (thanks Nohand).      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "DDMM[ Group Notes ]MMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMMDD    บ
 บ   3                                                                   3    บ
 บ   :    All groups make mistakes, and we made a big one by jumping the :    บ
 บ   :    gun on releasing GP2.  This release was an alpha, so we really :    บ
 บ   :    couldn't have fixed it.  Ohh yeah, and all you fargin lamers   :    บ
 บ   :    that pop in and out of our channel, fuck you.  You wouldn't    :    บ
 บ   :    have given 1/2 a shit if a well known group such as Prestige   :    บ
 บ   :    made a mistake like this.  Just because R2P is a new group,    :    บ
 บ   :    doesn't mean we're going to crumble from your idiotic pleas.   :    บ
 บ   :    R2P is here to stay.  R2P does all this for pure fun, the      :    บ
 บ   :    scene is not a full time job for us.  We are no longer going   :    บ
 บ   :    to listen your pathetic crying.  Go sit in a corner.           :    บ

 บ     The ratings listed above are judged in many categories.  1)            บ
 บ  Originality.  It has to be an idea unlike anyother.  2) Effectiveness.    บ
 บ  Is this a util that is helpful or just sits on a corner of your drive     บ
 บ  collecting dust?  3) Looks.  Let's face it, if it looks like shit, it     บ
 บ  probably is shit.  And last but not least, 4) Requirements.  I for one    บ
 บ  have a boring P100 with 16 MB RAM, I don't want to have to run out to     บ
 บ  CompUSA to get my ass RAM or a freaking DVD drive just to run a program   บ
 บ  I'm not going to use more than once!                                      บ

 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First some background, I by nature hate IRCops, period, sure they     บ
 บ  got a job to do, but so do me and my 10 clones.  Anyway, I enjoy and use  บ
 บ  smoke's clones whenever I feel it is necessary.  I am as careful as       บ
 บ  possible when cloning, making sure to span as many servers as possible,   บ
 บ  and to change nicks, etc.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway, there I was on a normal day, and some guy decides he can      บ
 บ  insult me, well I didn't have any transfers going on so I decided, hell   บ
 บ  let's load up the clones.  I load up each one by one, looking for a       บ
 บ  server I'm not k-lined on each time, I'm able to only have 1 clone on     บ
 บ  every server except irc.kern.com.  There, I was in my tempClone channel   บ
 บ  watching over them and doing my work, when in pops this dude named        บ
 บ  Moogle, he says "Clones are bad, we no like."  I was like get away, and   บ
 บ  kicked him promptly, he pops back in then I whois him noticing he is an   บ
 บ  IRCop, I say fuck off, and he K-lines 2 of my clones, (the ones on        บ
 บ  Kern).                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now I was pissed, what an ass, so I take my 7 remaining clones,       บ
 บ  start an all out attack, go get my 2 k-lined clones on different          บ
 บ  servers, and have them dcc bomb him.  And of course he went down, there   บ
 บ  I was laughing it off, then Boom like a gun shot me and each of my 9      บ
 บ  clones were instantly killed with the message "Don't flood me fucker" or  บ
 บ  something to that effect.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now I was furious, just cause he managed to type /kill he thinks he   บ
 บ  is hot shit, so I msg him asking what the fuck is up.  He starts being a  บ
 บ  total ass, so I start telling him off threatening him.  Then all of a     บ
 บ  sudden this happens:                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** oDogg^2 has quit IRC (Killed by Moogle, Threaten me some more,        บ
 บ  fucker)                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, MAYBE he was warranted to kill K-line my clones, maybe to kill   บ
 บ  them, but killing some one for threatening them sounds an awful lot like  บ
 บ  a #WarezX Channel.  Then I try to load up my clones and there are         บ
 บ  k-lines ALL over the place! W ith MSG's like: oDogg^2 You are banned      บ
 บ  from this server : bad_bad_bad_server_stuff.  Now what gives an IRCop    บ
 บ  the power to k-line ppl on multiple servers just for threatening, or      บ
 บ  just an isolated (as far as he knows) cloning incident!                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Odogg                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Dear Stupid Odoggy Dog,                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I have a few things to say about this, first, in the past few   บ
 บ  months I have made it my job to watch IRCops for bad kills, and try to    บ
 บ  get logs to publish and send to their admins.  AND in this time I have    บ
 บ  made some opers VERY pissed.  Right now, I can only log onto 3 servers,   บ
 บ  I logged on yesterday and found I was k-lined on anarchy for clones????   บ
 บ  I never ran clones there!  The opers do talk, and if you fuck with one    บ
 บ  expect to get fucked all over IRC.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BUT you can do other things to ops to annoy the shit outa them.       บ
 บ  When you see an OP kill someone for clones, message them and tell them    บ
 บ  what a nice kill that was, and how they must feel like a big man now,     บ
 บ  say like "WOW, you typed /KILL <Nick>, you must feel SOO POWERFUL.  This  บ
 บ  will almost ALWAYS piss a IRCop off BAD.  BUT they have NO RIGHT to kill  บ
 บ  you for this, that wasn't a threat.  And you weren't doing ANYTHING       บ
 บ  wrong.  If they kill you for that write it up and send it to me.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I once read one of the truest things ever when I started on the       บ
 บ  Internet.  I went to the MIRC Homepage and in BIG TYPE it said, STAY      บ
 บ  AWAY FROM OPS THEY ARE THE SCUM OF THE IRC, AND ARE JUST KIDS WITH        บ
 บ  POWER.  And I have seen this proven true for about %95 of IRCops.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ

 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC, channel operators, and the warez scene.  It goes hand in hand,   บ
 บ  yet they clash horribly at times.  IRC is obviously great for warez in    บ
 บ  some ways.  I would probably never be involved without it, since there    บ
 บ  are none of those 'k-rad elite boards' out here.  But shit, IRC brings    บ
 บ  out the lamest in some people, and most ops don't help it at all.  I'm    บ
 บ  just kinda writing a list of things that bug me, and why they do.  So     บ
 บ  here it is :                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <WaReZd0oD> I want Command & Conquer, and Warcraft II, and MS Office      บ
 บ              95!!!                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Fro> Yeah, I got Command & Conquer, 12 disks, wanna trade?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <WaReZd0oD> Sure!!  Do you want a site list??                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Fro> No, but do you have .A03, A07, and .A16 of Dark Forces?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <WaReZd0oD> What's an .A03 file?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Fro> Woops!  Gotta go!!                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is an extreme example obviously, but still, I've seen stuff      บ
 บ  like this happen.  It's more often new guys, who are looking for good     บ
 บ  stuff to trade, but still, take that site list you have, open your damn   บ
 บ  cute FTP, and search through the list.  Find one small thing on each      บ
 บ  site you like, and download it.  Upload your list, or whatever you        บ
 บ  downloaded from the last site.  Share the warez!!                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's really nice when you go out for a pop and you leave a timer in   บ
 บ  your home channel telling everyone that, but when some schmuch types      บ
 บ  /timer 999 60 /me wants Virtual Valerie!!  Then the ass leaves his        บ
 บ  computer and goes to sleep.  By the time he wakes up, most of the people  บ
 บ  who messaged him will be gone, so he's wasted his time, our time,         บ
 บ  bandwidth, and generally made an ass of himself.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have on ONE occasion used a timer, it was in #warez666 on           บ
 บ  UnderNet, and it was set at 5 minutes.  Everyone who joins the channel    บ
 บ  will likely see that once, and once they've seen it once and said to      บ
 บ  themselves "Nope, I don't have that for him," they just want to get on    บ
 บ  with their trading, not see your request every minute.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are times you REALLY need some software, or a crack, or         บ
 บ  whatever.  But don't put a timer on.  Check the fileservers, the XDCC     บ
 บ  lists, and the sites.  Then ask, but damn, don't put a timer on!  With    บ
 บ  mIRC, just hit the damn up arrow to repeat your last command, and do it   บ
 บ  every couple of minutes randomly.  That way, you can make sure your       บ
 บ  message gets out when there is less scrolling text obscuring it.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Ops that don't follow their own rules really bother me.  When an op   บ
 บ  starts to flood, repeat, and any of that shit, they don't deserve ops.    บ
 บ  One example last week was an op flooding the channel with his request.    บ
 บ  Ok, so I can put up with that for a few seconds, but he went on and on.   บ
 บ  And his request was fucking for shareware!!  Finally, I sent it to him,   บ
 บ  and got a thanks, which was really appreaciated.  If you are going to     บ
 บ  make a rule, be prepared to follow it!  Same goes to non-ops, follow the  บ
 บ  unwritten channel rules and you will get along just fine.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm by no means Elite, nor do I claim to be.  I'm an ordinary warez   บ
 บ  leech who passes between 5-15 megs through his computer a day, and is     บ
 บ  sick of all the bullshit that is ruining the scene.  When I started       บ
 บ  about 6 months ago, it was bad, but not this bad.  Enough bitching,       บ
 บ  great mag!                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Fro                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
