 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Crack                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Hacker's Corner #1                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I will tell you how to get FREE Cokes.  I know it's nothing big, but  บ
 บ  still, it's FREE.  This trick only works on COCA COLA machines.  It has   บ
 บ  something to do with the validator on the machines. 										 Take a     บ
 บ  dollar bill (as crisp as possible) and lay it george-side-up with our     บ
 บ  dear first prez.  Face it left as if you were going to stick it in the    บ
 บ  machine.  Now take some scotch tape and make 2 strips as long as the      บ
 บ  dollar.  Now take those pieces of tape and attach them to the white edge  บ
 บ  of the dollar facing you (just the one edge).  Your dollar should look    บ
 บ  like this now.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                            --------                                        บ
 บ                            -      -                                        บ
 บ                            -      - <=---Tape                              บ
 บ                            -      -                                        บ
 บ                            -      -                                        บ
 บ                            +------+                                        บ
 บ                            |      |                                        บ
 บ                            |      | <=---Dollar                            บ
 บ                            |      |                                        บ
 บ                            |      |                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now take scotch tape and make bars across the two pieces of tape      บ
 บ  already connected to your dollar (sort of like a ladder) overlapping      บ
 บ  each one just a little.  Get down to the bottom and turn the bill over    บ
 บ  and do the same thing on the other side (just the ladder rungs).  Now     บ
 บ  take a pair of scissors and trim the tape to make it all even and         บ
 บ  square.  Now take something hard and run it over the tape a few times to  บ
 บ  ensure that it won't come off (Remember kindergarten?  Put the glue on    บ
 บ  and press down hard while you count to 10?).  Now you're ready.  Take     บ
 บ  your new and improved currency to the nearest coke machine with a dollar  บ
 บ  bill vindicator and insert your dollar.  You have to let the bill go in   บ
 บ  almost until you cant hold the tape anymore, it's important to let the    บ
 บ  bill get in far enough for the scanner to read the dollar, and then whip  บ
 บ  it back out.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You should hear the click of the machine and your change drop out.    บ
 บ  Make your selection and voila!  Now the cool thing is when you find a     บ
 บ  machine that only takes 50 cents.  Cause you get your coke and 50 cents.  บ
 บ  I made 300 dollars one time doing that.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Another Way :                                                             บ
 บ  -------------                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Take two dollar bills, one facing george-side-up, and the other       บ
 บ  facing george-side-down.  Take a piece of CLEAR tape, and tape them       บ
 บ  together.  Make sure NO space is between the two bills.  Now go to the    บ
 บ  nearest machine, and insert the bills.  It should go in enough to read    บ
 บ  the first bill.  Then when it reads the second bill, thinking you want    บ
 บ  two cokes, it rejects the bill since the second bill is                   บ
 บ  george-side-down.  When it rejects, the first dollar comes with it.  You  บ
 บ  get your coke, and maybe some change.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Another Way :                                                             บ
 บ  -------------                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This method is probably the easiest because it requires no            บ
 บ  preparation!  Go to a vending machine and pretend you are putting in a    บ
 บ  dollar bill, push the button of the coke you want, keep pressing it.      บ
 บ  Then yell out a swear, go to the store manager, and tell them the         บ
 บ  machine ate your money, they get a coke for you, you thank them, they     บ
 บ  apologize, you go away to another store, and you do the same thing.  If   บ
 บ  you want the money, then follow the procedures, and when it comes to the  บ
 บ  store manager, tell them the machine ate your money, and when they say    บ
 บ  they'll get you a new one, say no, I have to go, I want my money back.    บ
 บ  Then you get money.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A combination of the two is good too.  Go to one store, tell them     บ
 บ  you want a coke, because it ate your money, then go to another store,     บ
 บ  tell them you want money back, then go to another store, you want coke,   บ
 บ  another, money, etc.  This way, you get coke, and money to get more coke  บ
 บ  or other things like jewelry for your girlfriend or computer stuff.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Another Way :                                                             บ
 บ  -------------                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If the machine only accepts coins, then you're in luck, have I got a  บ
 บ  ripping job for you!  Get a train schedule, go to the rail road tracks 5  บ
 บ  minutes before the train comes.  Bring loads of nickels, put them on the  บ
 บ  rail road track.  Wait until the train runs them over. You should now     บ
 บ  see a flat piece of metal in the place of the nickel.  Notice how its     บ
 บ  the same size has a quarter?  Now use it.  Get 1 can of coke for 15       บ
 บ  cents, instead of 75 cents.  Oh yeah, if you're not careful, the train    บ
 บ  might run over you legs, OUCH!  So, do becareful out there.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      Test your knowledge of the WAREZ SCENE!  The following are TEN mind   บ
 บ  boggling "YOU DON'T KNOW NOTHIN'" questions!  Enter all your answers in,  บ
 บ  and when you feel you're happy with them, press F10 and the computer      บ
 บ  will tally up your score and spit it out at you.  For every question you  บ
 บ  missed, the computer will indicate the correct answer.  Oh, and if you    บ
 บ  feel like "You Don't Know Nothin'" midway through the quiz and don't      บ
 บ  want to embarrass yourself with an incredibly low score, press ESC and    บ
 บ  you'll be back on the bright side of RCN, the awesome music will calm     บ
 บ  you down, and all will be well again.. enjoy!                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* All answers are found in issues of RCN!                              บ

                              ฐ฿฿฿฿฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Dark-Elf and Amy, Amy Replies!!!                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So apparently Rebel Chicken's letter to Emily inspired other young    บ
 บ  chickens (or Elves as the case may be) to write letters via email to      บ
 บ  THEIR girls, or girls-to-be.  Recently on IRC I had Dark-Elf online and   บ
 บ  he said he had just e-mailed this girl he really liked.  Well, that's     บ
 บ  legit.  Then, he asked me to publish it in RCN because he wanted to show  บ
 บ  his girl how famous he is.  Fair enough.  So here it is, the unedited,    บ
 บ  unabridged version. Enjoy.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Amy,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      How's your summer so far?  Mine has been good.  How has yours been    บ
 บ  so far? [Getting a tad repetitive here Dark!?]  Do you like school?  Or   บ
 บ  do you like going to school?  I like going to school because that's       บ
 บ  where all my friends are.  I liked being around you in school.  I miss    บ
 บ  being around you.  [Golly gee how sweet!]  Well so far this summer.  I    บ
 บ  went to the movies a couple times with my best friend, (Stephen).  I      บ
 บ  went to ultra-zone a lot.  I am a role-player at ultra-zone (I am proud)  บ
 บ  [well sure Dark, I would be too!].  Role-players are the best people at   บ
 บ  ultra-zone.  I have some good places.  We are going on vacation on July,  บ
 บ  4 1996.  We will be gone for 2 weeks to Florida.  Maybe we can go to the  บ
 บ  movies sometime.  We could just like meet there at the movie theatre.     บ
 บ  If you do not want to then don't.  Don't say yes because you can't say    บ
 บ  no [Dark, one thing you will find about women, is that they NEVER say     บ
 บ  Yes when they mean No!].  Say yes if you mean it.  If you know what I     บ
 บ  mean.  If you have a boyfriend now I shall understand.  Life's like a     บ
 บ  box of choclates [pffffft!!!].  You never know what you're going to get.  บ
 บ  Well this is a little guess into a box of choclates.  As to if you would  บ
 บ  like to spend some time with me [not original but kinda cute I guess!].   บ
 บ  If you don't wanna go to movies.  We can go to ultra-zone.  I shall       บ
 บ  protect you there [BUAAAAAAHAHAHAHA!!!].  It will be alot of fun for me   บ
 บ  wherever we go.  If you feel you are in commitment with that farmer guy   บ
 บ  [ooh, that may have cost you the medal right there!]?  Then don't go out  บ
 บ  with me. Especially a person I don not even know.  This letter was        บ
 บ  semi-hard to write, because I did not know the out come of the            บ
 บ  reader(You).  I tried to give it to you in school but I could not [cuz    บ
 บ  I'm a whimp].  All these mixed emotions!  It's hard being a TeenAge boy   บ
 บ  [HAHAHAHAAH!!!].  Please don't show this letter to anyone [hmm.. now I'm  บ
 บ  confused].  If you ask me if you can show it to them then I shall give    บ
 บ  ya an answer.  If PJ wants to read it she can (she is your best friend).  บ
 บ  She really does not like me as a friend though.  I just think me and PJ   บ
 บ  think differently.  Just wanted her know that.  Remember.  You mean Yes   บ
 บ  or You mean No.  Gimme an answer tha'ts in your heart for there is an     บ
 บ  answer to any question in the universe. [roo!?]                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The time is 1:43am 6-20-96.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I write things real late because tha'ts when all my feelings come     บ
 บ  out.  I usually go to sleep earlier though.  Hope you feel the same way   บ
 บ  I do about you as you do me [see comments below!].  If you don't then     บ
 บ  say now.  It will be ok.  If you do please tell me.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Love,                        บ
 บ                                                  Dark-Elf                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My my my... MYYYYY my my.  MYYYYYYYYYYY my my my!  Well Dark-Elf, I   บ
 บ  really hope for the best.  Hope being the key word in that sentence.  So  บ
 บ  I have a few things to say.  First of all, how the FUCK are you going to  บ
 บ  "protect" Amy at ultra-zone!?  Second, what IS ultra-zone!?  Third, next  บ
 บ  time you write a girl a letter, run it through one of the RCN Editors     บ
 บ  first, we'll fix all the grammar ;-).  And lastly, let me just comment    บ
 บ  on the sentence "Hope you feel the same way I do about you as you do      บ
 บ  me."  There's a very important thing when writing a letter to a girl for  บ
 บ  the first time.  You HAVE to make sure that the romantic part of the      บ
 บ  letter says exactly what you meant for it to say.  The small-talk         บ
 บ  doesn't matter too much, it just burns space on the paper, it's the       บ
 บ  leading action, but your climax can't say something you didn't mean for   บ
 บ  it to.  Let me first explain what that sentence means, in reality.  It    บ
 บ  means that you hope she feels the same things you feel for her as she     บ
 บ  "does" your or, as your average girl would understand, as she has sex     บ
 บ  with you.  My my my, on a first letter, this is NOT what you want to      บ
 บ  say!  So next time, write something more to the effect of "I hope you     บ
 บ  feel the same way about me as I feel about you."  Anyway, good luck, and  บ
 บ  remember, our thoughts are with you.  Uh oh.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  A week has passed and here's Amy's reply!                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Paul (Dark-Elf),                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm doing fine.  I have to tell you I was quite surprised when I      บ
 บ  read you letter.  Thank you for being so completely honest with me.  It   บ
 บ  makes things much easier; so I owe it to you to be completely honest.  I  บ
 บ  don't really have a commitment with farmer Michael.  The way we left      บ
 บ  things it was unsaid.  I don't have a boyfriend right now.  Paul, I like  บ
 บ  you a lot as a friend.  I know you hate hearing that.  I think you're     บ
 บ  funny, sweet, and cute, but not just that way.  I would, however, like    บ
 บ  to hang out with you sometime.  Going to the movies would be fun. I'm     บ
 บ  not saying yes because I can't say no and I'm giving you the answer that  บ
 บ  is in my heart.  I think it is equally hard being a teenage girl.  I do   บ
 บ  love the way you write letters.  You are very funny (in a good way).  I   บ
 บ  really had no idea you felt that way.  Please write me back and tell me   บ
 บ  your feelings on all of this.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Love,                        บ
 บ                                                  Amy                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Dark-Elf.. my my my!!  Well what can I say?  You've expected the      บ
 บ  unexpected and it happened!  So she's not in love with you but she wants  บ
 บ  to go out.  Now do you have the balls to ask her?!  Hey, that's a better  บ
 บ  reply than what Rebel Chicken got when he wrote Emily!                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      RCN is proud to present to the scene the official RCN t-shirt.  We    บ
 บ  tried to keep the price as low as we could so that everyone can enjoy     บ
 บ  these goodies.  Keeping with RCN's volunteerish spirit to help the scene, บ
 บ  Road Rebel has decided to take it upon himself to make the RCN t-shirts   บ
 บ  available to the masses.  This is a non-profit venture and we hope that   บ
 บ  in many ways, RCN continues to benefit the scene.. even when we are not   บ
 บ  near our computers.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The RCN logo is approximately 8"x6" printed on the back of a        บ
 บ        HEAVY-duty Fruit of the Loom white t-shirt, the front is plain.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       A preview of the shirt can viewed upon pressing escape.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Special orders take up to 4 weeks for shipping.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Summary :                                                                 บ
 บ  ---------                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) All RCN issues must be online and available for FREE download.  The   บ
 บ      current issue and back issues must be located in separate file        บ
 บ      directories.  The FULL file_id.diz for the current issue must be      บ
 บ      shown.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) A "Reality Check Network" conference must be set up.  The "rcn        บ
 บ      affiliate board" ansi must be shown somewhere in the login process    บ
 บ      or somewhere in the conference join.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Sysops must notify all bulletin board users, via nonconference        บ
 บ      specific mass email, of the new issues available for free download.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The new update to the Reality Check Network World Wide Web Site,      บ
 บ  http://www.rcn.org/, adds many new features :                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Speed Optimization : RCN.org is now speed optimized, which means    บ
 บ        you spend less time waiting and more time browsing.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Back Issue Access : It's now quick and easy to scan through  บ
 บ        RCN's back issues, each one has its full description online, to     บ
 บ        make searching for the desired issue that much easier.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Interface : v2.0 brings an end to the confusing              บ
 บ        conglomeration of pages that previously had existed.  Now speed     บ
 บ        through the icon driven interface to scan back issues of RCN and    บ
 บ        other emags, send comments, read credits, and check out             บ
 บ        merchandise and free files.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Text or JAVA Version : Whatever browser you use can now access the  บ
 บ        RCN.org pages.  Before only Netscape was allowed, but now LYNX and  บ
 บ        other text base users can now access the pages.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       New Look Graphics : The new graphics style are a nice change of     บ
 บ        pace from the hard-edged style of before.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a file mirror, contact us in #RCN on IRC, you must be able  บ
 บ  to store all back issues in a publically accessible directory from the    บ
 บ  WWW.  A link will be created from RCN.org to your site, so users can      บ
 บ  acquire issues from there if the main site becomes overloaded.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN WWW Site       : http://www.rcn.org/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN Mirror Site #1 : http://www.halcyon.com/sbecker                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
